pThe bDenver Nuggetsb are an American professional basketball team based in a hrefwikiDenver titleDenverDenver Coloradoa. The Nuggets compete in the a hrefwikiNationalBasketballAssociation titleNational Basketball AssociationNational Basketball Associationa NBA as a member club of the leagues a hrefwikiWesternConferenceNBA titleWestern Conference NBAWestern Conferencea a hrefwikiNorthwestDivisionNBA titleNorthwest Division NBANorthwest Divisiona. The team was founded as the bDenver Larksb in 1967 as a charter franchise of the a hrefwikiAmericanBasketballAssociation titleAmerican Basketball AssociationAmerican Basketball Associationa ABA but changed its name to bRocketsb before the first season.sup idciteref9 classreferencea hrefcitenote991993asup It changed its name again to the Nuggets in 1974.sup idciteref10 classreferencea hrefcitenote10911093asup After the name change the Nuggets played for the final a hrefwikiListofABAchampions titleList of ABA championsABA Championshipa title in 1976 losing to the a hrefwikiNewYorkNets classmwredirect titleNew York NetsNew York Netsa.
ppThe team has had some periods of success qualifying for the ABA Playoffs for all seasons from 1967 to the a hrefwiki1976ABAplayoffs classmwredirect title1976 ABA playoffs1976 ABA playoffsa where it lost in the finals.sup idciterefbasketballreference110 classreferencea hrefcitenotebasketballreference11911193asup The team joined the NBA in 1976 after the a hrefwikiAmericanBasketballAssociationE28093NationalBasketballAssociationmerger classmwredirect titleAmerican Basketball AssociationNational Basketball Association mergerABANBA mergera and qualified for the a hrefwikiNBAplayoffs titleNBA playoffsNBA playoffsa in nine consecutive seasons in the 1980s and ten consecutive seasons from 2004 to 2013.sup idciterefbasketballreference111 classreferencea hrefcitenotebasketballreference11911193asup However it has not made an appearance in a a hrefwikiNBAFinals titleNBA Finalschampionship rounda since its last year in the ABA.sup idciterefbasketballreference112 classreferencea hrefcitenotebasketballreference11911193asup The Nuggets play their home games at a hrefwikiPepsiCenter titlePepsi CenterPepsi Centera which they share with the a hrefwikiColoradoAvalanche titleColorado AvalancheColorado Avalanchea of the a hrefwikiNationalHockeyLeague titleNational Hockey LeagueNational Hockey Leaguea NHL and the a hrefwikiColoradoMammoth titleColorado MammothColorado Mammotha of the a hrefwikiNationalLacrosseLeague titleNational Lacrosse LeagueNational Lacrosse Leaguea NLL.
p

h2span classmwheadline idFranchisehistoryFranchise historyspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection1 titleEdit section Franchise historyeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh2
h3span id1948.E2.80.931950Originalrunspanspan classmwheadline id19481950Originalrun19481950 Original runspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection2 titleEdit section 19481950 Original runeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pThe a hrefwikiDenverNuggets1948E2809350 titleDenver Nuggets 194850original Denver Nuggetsa was founded in the a hrefwikiNationalBasketballLeagueUnitedStates titleNational Basketball League United StatesNational Basketball Leaguea prior to the 194849 season. Following that season the NBL was absorbed into the BAA which was then renamed to the a hrefwikiNBA classmwredirect titleNBANBAa. The Denver Nuggets played the a hrefwiki1949E2809350NBAseason title194950 NBA season194950 seasona as one of the charter NBA teams before folding.
p
h3span classmwheadline idTheDenverRocketsandABArevivalThe Denver Rockets and ABA revivalspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection3 titleEdit section The Denver Rockets and ABA revivaleditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pIn 1967 one of the ABAs charter franchises was awarded to a group in a hrefwikiKansasCityMissouri titleKansas City MissouriKansas City Missouria headed by Southern Californian businessman James Trindle. However Trindle was unable to find a suitable arena in the Kansas City area. League commissioner a hrefwikiGeorgeMikan titleGeorge MikanGeorge Mikana suggested moving the team to Denver. After agreeing to name Denver resident and former NBA player a hrefwikiVinceBoryla titleVince BorylaVince Borylaa as general manager Trindle moved his team to Denver as the Denver Larks named after Colorados state bird.sup idciterefnuggetscompanyhistory120 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggetscompanyhistory12911293asup The Trindle group was severely undercapitalized leading Mikan to order the Larks to post a 100000 performance bond or lose the franchise. Hours before the deadline Trindle sold a  controlling interest to Denver trucking magnate Bill Ringsby for 350000. Ringsby then renamed the team the Rockets after his companys longhaul trucks.sup idciteref13 classreferencea hrefcitenote13911393asup
p
h3span id1969.E2.80.931976ABAyearsspanspan classmwheadline id19691976ABAyears19691976 ABA yearsspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection4 titleEdit section 19691976 ABA yearseditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pPlaying at the a hrefwikiDenverAuditoriumArena titleDenver Auditorium ArenaDenver Auditorium Arenaa the Rockets had early successes on the court developing a solid fan base along the way.sup idciterefremembertheaba.com140 classreferencea hrefcitenoteremembertheaba.com14911493asup However the team had a history of early playoff exits and failed to play in an ABA championship series.
ppEarly they had a solid lineup led by a hrefwikiByronBeck titleByron BeckByron Becka and a hrefwikiLarryJonesbasketball titleLarry Jones basketballLarry Jonesa then later by Beck and a hrefwikiRalphSimpson titleRalph SimpsonRalph Simpsona. a hrefwikiLonnieWright titleLonnie WrightLonnie Wrighta of the a hrefwikiAmericanFootballLeague titleAmerican Football LeagueAmerican Football Leagueas a hrefwikiDenverBroncos titleDenver BroncosDenver Broncosa signed with the Rockets during that first season and became the first player to play professional football and basketball in the same season. Wright played four seasons with Denver.sup idciterefremembertheaba.com141 classreferencea hrefcitenoteremembertheaba.com14911493asup Controversial rookie a hrefwikiSpencerHaywood titleSpencer HaywoodSpencer Haywooda joined the team for the 196970 season. Haywood was one of the first players to turn pro before graduating from college and the NBA initially refused to let him play in the league. Haywood averaged nearly 30 points and 19.5 rebounds per game in his only ABA season being named ABA MVP ABA rookie of the year as well as the AllStar Game MVP. The team finished 5133 winning their division before exiting the playoffs in the 2nd round.
ppJust before the start of the 197071 season Haywood signed with the a hrefwikiSeattleSuperSonics titleSeattle SuperSonicsSeattle SuperSonicsa jumping to the NBA. The team tumbled to a 3054 record and attendance suffered.sup idciterefremembertheaba.com142 classreferencea hrefcitenoteremembertheaba.com14911493asup
p
h4span classmwheadline idBecomingtheDenverNuggetsBecoming the Denver Nuggetsspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection5 titleEdit section Becoming the Denver Nuggetseditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh4
pRingsby sold the team to a hrefwikiSanDiego titleSan DiegoSan Diegoa businessmen Frank Goldberg and Bud Fischer in 1972.sup idciterefnuggetscompanyhistory121 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggetscompanyhistory12911293asup In 1974 in anticipation of moving into the a hrefwikiNationalBasketballAssociation titleNational Basketball AssociationNBAa and the new a hrefwikiMcNicholsArena classmwredirect titleMcNichols ArenaMcNichols Arenaa the franchise held a contest to choose a new team nickname as Rockets was already in use by the a hrefwikiHoustonRockets titleHouston RocketsHouston Rocketsa. The winning choice was Nuggets in honor of the original a hrefwikiDenverNuggetsoriginal classmwredirect titleDenver Nuggets originalNuggetsa team in Denver from 194850 the last year as a charter member of the NBA. Their new logo was a miner discovering an ABA ball. Goldberg and Fischer in turn sold the team to a local investment group in 1976.
ppWith the drafting and signing of future hall of fame player a hrefwikiDavidThompsonbasketball titleDavid Thompson basketballDavid Thompsona out of a hrefwikiNCStateWolfpackmen27sbasketball titleNC State Wolfpack men39s basketballNorth Carolina Statea a hrefwikiMarvinWebster titleMarvin WebsterMarvin Webstera and the acquisitions of a hrefwikiDanIssel titleDan IsselDan Issela and a hrefwikiBobbyJonesbasketballborn1951 titleBobby Jones basketball born 1951Bobby Jonesa and with a hrefwikiLarryBrownbasketball titleLarry Brown basketballLarry Browna coaching they had their best seasons in team history in their first two seasons as the Nuggets. Playing in the a hrefwikiDenverAuditoriumArena titleDenver Auditorium ArenaDenver Auditorium Arenaa for the last season the 197475 team went 6516 including a 402 record at home. However a quick playoff exit followed.sup idciterefReferenceA150 classreferencea hrefcitenoteReferenceA15911593asup
ppIn 197576 playing at their new arena the Nuggets edged the reigning champion a hrefwikiKentuckyColonels titleKentucky ColonelsKentucky Colonelsa four games to three to make the a hrefwiki1976ABAPlayoffs title1976 ABA Playoffs1976 ABA finalsa for the first time. Eventually they lost to the a hrefwikiNewYorkNets classmwredirect titleNew York NetsNew York Netsa and a hrefwikiJuliusErving titleJulius ErvingJulius Ervinga.sup idciterefReferenceA151 classreferencea hrefcitenoteReferenceA15911593asup They did not get a second chance to win an ABA league championship as the a hrefwikiAmericanBasketballAssociationE28093NationalBasketballAssociationmerger classmwredirect titleAmerican Basketball AssociationNational Basketball Association mergerABANBA mergera took place after the 197576 season. The Nuggets Nets a hrefwikiIndianaPacers titleIndiana PacersIndiana Pacersa and a hrefwikiSanAntonioSpurs titleSan Antonio SpursSan Antonio Spursa were merged into the NBA. The a hrefwikiSpiritsofSt.Louis titleSpirits of St. LouisSpirits of St. Louisa and Kentucky Colonels were disbanded.sup idciteref16 classreferencea hrefcitenote16911693asup
p
h3span id1976.E2.80.931982EarlyNBAyearsspanspan classmwheadline id19761982EarlyNBAyears19761982 Early NBA yearsspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection6 titleEdit section 19761982 Early NBA yearseditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pThe Nuggets and Nets had actually applied to join the NBA in 1975 but were forced to stay in the ABA by a court order. The Nuggets continued their strong play early on in the NBA as they won division titles in their first two seasons in the league and missed a third by a single game. However neither of these teams were ultimately successful in the postseason. Similarly to the other new NBA teams the Nuggets were given many financial issues including a 2 million entry fee. a hrefwikiRedMcCombs titleRed McCombsRed McCombsa bought the team in 1978.
ppIn 1979 Brown left the team helping usher in a brief decline in their teams performance. It ended in 1981 when they hired a hrefwikiDougMoe titleDoug MoeDoug Moea as a head coach. Moe brought with him a motion offense philosophy a style of play focusing on attempting to move the ball until someone got open. Moe was also known for not paying as much attention to defense as his colleagues. The offense helped the team become highly competitive. During the 1980s the Nuggets oftensup classnoprint InlineTemplate TemplateFact stylewhitespacenowrap91ia hrefwikiWikipediaManualofStyleDatesandnumbers titleWikipediaManual of StyleDates and numbersspan titleThis term requires quantification. June 2015quantifyspanai93sup scored in excess of 115 points a game and during the 198182 season they scored at least 100 points in every game. The NBArecord streak was halted at 136 consecutive games.sup idciterefNBARecords170 classreferencea hrefcitenoteNBARecords17911793asup During the 198182 season the Nuggets set the league scoring record for the highest points per game average at 126.5 points.
p
h3span id1982.E2.80.931989TheAlexEnglisheraspanspan classmwheadline id19821989TheAlexEnglishera19821989 The Alex English eraspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection7 titleEdit section 19821989 The Alex English eraeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pAnchored by scoring machines a hrefwikiAlexEnglish titleAlex EnglishAlex Englisha and a hrefwikiKikiVandeweghe classmwredirect titleKiki VandewegheKiki Vandeweghea at the two forward spots and Dan Issel at center Denver led the league in scoring with English and Vandeweghe both averaging above 25 points per game. It was a novel strategy allowing the Nuggets to top the Midwest Division and qualify for the playoffs during that span. On December 13 1983 the Nuggets and the visiting a hrefwikiDetroitPistons titleDetroit PistonsDetroit Pistonsa combined for an NBA record 370 points with Detroit winning in triple a hrefwikiOvertimesportBasketball classmwredirect titleOvertime sportovertimea 186184. At the end of the season English won the NBA scoring title becoming the only Nugget to win the award despite the heavily favored offensive play of Doug Moe. In a hrefwiki1984E2809385NBAseason title198485 NBA season198485a they made it to the a hrefwikiWesternConferenceNBA titleWestern Conference NBAWestern Conferencea finals after being perennial playoff contenders and they lost in 5 games to the a hrefwikiLosAngelesLakers titleLos Angeles LakersLos Angeles Lakersa.
ppVandeweghe was traded before the 198485 season to the a hrefwikiPortlandTrailBlazers titlePortland Trail BlazersPortland Trail Blazersa for 63 rebounding guard a hrefwikiFatLever titleFat LeverFat Levera undersized power forward a hrefwikiCalvinNatt titleCalvin NattCalvin Natta and center a hrefwikiWayneCooperbasketball titleWayne Cooper basketballWayne Coopera. Spearheaded by Alex English and supported by the three new acquisitions and defensive specialists a hrefwikiBillHanzlik titleBill HanzlikBill Hanzlika and a hrefwikiTRDunn classmwredirect titleTR DunnTR Dunna the team replicated its success in the Western Conference despite the loss of Vandeweghe. They even managed to win 54 games in the a hrefwiki1987E2809388NBAseason title198788 NBA season198788 seasona the most they had ever won as an NBA team. However the Mavericks eliminated the Nuggets in the second round of the 1988 NBA Playoffs. McCombs sold the team to a hrefwikiSidneyShlenker titleSidney ShlenkerSidney Shlenkera in 1985. Shlenker in turn sold the team to a hrefwikiCOMSAT titleCOMSATCOMSATa in 1989.
p
h3span id1989.E2.80.931991Aperiodofdeclinespanspan classmwheadline id19891991Aperiodofdecline19891991 A period of declinespanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection8 titleEdit section 19891991 A period of declineeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pMoe left the team in 1990 and was replaced by a hrefwikiPaulWesthead titlePaul WestheadPaul Westheada. Westhead also believed in a a hrefwikiRunandgunbasketball titleRun and gun basketballrun and guna style of play and gave the green light for players like a hrefwikiMichaelAdamsbasketball titleMichael Adams basketballMichael Adamsa and a hrefwikiMahmoudAbdulRauf titleMahmoud AbdulRaufChris Jacksona to light up the scoreboards within seconds of possession.
p
div classthumb trightdiv classthumbinner stylewidth172pxa hrefwikiFileLipofskyDikembeMutombo.jpg classimageimg alt srcupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumbaa6LipofskyDikembeMutombo.jpg170pxLipofskyDikembeMutombo.jpg decodingasync width170 height161 classthumbimage srcsetupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumbaa6LipofskyDikembeMutombo.jpg255pxLipofskyDikembeMutombo.jpg 1.5x upload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsaa6LipofskyDikembeMutombo.jpg 2x datafilewidth300 datafileheight284 a  div classthumbcaptiondiv classmagnifya hrefwikiFileLipofskyDikembeMutombo.jpg classinternal titleEnlargeadivDikembe Mutombo shown with the 76ers was drafted by the Nuggets in 1991.divdivdiv
pHowever Westhead cared even less about defense than Moe. As a result the Nuggets gave up points so quickly that even their prolific offense could not 
keep up. They finished with the worst record in the league during the 199091 season despite setting many scoring records. As an insult many sportswriters nicknamed the team at the time as the Enver Nuggets as in no D or no defense.
p
h3span id1991.E2.80.931996TheDikembeMutomboeraspanspan classmwheadline id19911996TheDikembeMutomboera19911996 The Dikembe Mutombo eraspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection9 titleEdit section 19911996 The Dikembe Mutombo eraeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pDenver took a positive step in rebuilding by drafting a hrefwikiGeorgetownHoyasmen27sbasketball titleGeorgetown Hoyas men39s basketballGeorgetown Universitya center a hrefwikiDikembeMutombo titleDikembe MutomboDikembe Mutomboa in 1991. Mutombo finished runnerup to a hrefwikiLarryJohnsonbasketballborn1969 titleLarry Johnson basketball born 1969Larry Johnsona for the NBA rookie of the year that season. Denver finished 2458 that year.
ppDenver fired Westhead prior to the 199293 season and hired former star player a hrefwikiDanIssel titleDan IsselDan Issela as his successor. The Nuggets had two lottery picks that year and drafted a hrefwikiNotreDameFightingIrishmen27sbasketball titleNotre Dame Fighting Irish men39s basketballUniversity of Notre Damea a hrefwikiForwardbasketball classmwredirect titleForward basketballforwarda a hrefwikiLaPhonsoEllis titleLaPhonso EllisLaPhonso Ellisa and a hrefwikiVirginiaCavaliersmen27sbasketball titleVirginia Cavaliers men39s basketballUniversity of Virginiaa a hrefwikiGuardbasketball classmwredirect titleGuard basketballguarda a hrefwikiBryantStith titleBryant StithBryant Stitha. Denver improved to 3646 just missing the playoffs that year.
ppDenver ditched their rainbow colors for a dark navy metallic gold and wine color scheme starting in the 199394 season. Led by Mutombo a hrefwikiMahmoudAbdulRauf titleMahmoud AbdulRaufMahmoud AbdulRaufa who changed his name from Chris Jackson prior to the season and Ellis Denver finished with its first winning season since the Doug Moe era at 4240. Denver clinched the 8th seed in the Western Conference playoffs playing the first place a hrefwikiSeattleSuperSonics titleSeattle SuperSonicsSeattle SuperSonicsa. Denver was a heavy underdog having only a couple of players on their roster with actual NBA playoff experience. After dropping the first two games of the fivegame set in a hrefwikiSeattle titleSeattleSeattlea the series returned to Denver. Denver won both games and tied the series at 2. The Nuggets made NBA history in Game 5 upsetting Seattle in overtime 9894. They became the first 8thseeded team to defeat a 1stseeded team in NBA playoff history. Denver almost repeated the feat before falling to the a hrefwikiUtahJazz titleUtah JazzUtah Jazza in Game 7 of the second round.
ppDenver acquired Sonics sharpshooter a hrefwikiDaleEllis titleDale EllisDale Ellisa in the offseason and drafted a hrefwikiMichiganWolverinesmen27sbasketball titleMichigan Wolverines men39s basketballUniversity of Michigana guard a hrefwikiJalenRose titleJalen RoseJalen Rosea. Denver struggled causing Issel to resign as coach partway into the season. Assistant Coach a hrefwikiGeneLittles titleGene LittlesGene Littlesa assumed control for a brief period before relinquishing control to general manager a hrefwikiBernieBickerstaff titleBernie BickerstaffBernie Bickerstaffa. Denver rebounded and earned the 8th seed again in the playoffs finishing 4141. The Nuggets were swept by the a hrefwikiSanAntonioSpurs titleSan Antonio SpursSan Antonio Spursa in the first round of the playoffs that season.
ppFollowing that season Denver acquired a hrefwikiAntonioMcDyess titleAntonio McDyessAntonio McDyessa in a draft day trade with the a hrefwikiLosAngelesClippers titleLos Angeles ClippersLos Angeles Clippersa. McDyess was the face of the franchise for the next few years as Mutombo left after the 199596 season for the a hrefwikiAtlantaHawks titleAtlanta HawksAtlanta Hawksa Ellis missed the majority of the next few seasons due to recurring knee and leg injuries Rose was traded to the a hrefwikiIndianaPacers titleIndiana PacersIndiana Pacersa for a hrefwikiMarkJacksonbasketball titleMark Jackson basketballMark Jacksona and AbdulRauf was traded to the a hrefwikiSacramentoKings titleSacramento KingsSacramento Kingsa prior to the 199697 season.
p
h3span id1997.E2.80.932003Anotherperiodofstrugglespanspan classmwheadline id19972003Anotherperiodofstruggle19972003 Another period of strugglespanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection10 titleEdit section 19972003 Another period of struggleeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pAfter finishing the 199697 season with the fourth worst record in the league 2161 the Nuggets sent a hrefwikiAntonioMcDyess titleAntonio McDyessAntonio McDyessa to the a hrefwikiPhoenixSuns titlePhoenix SunsPhoenix Sunsa and a hrefwikiDaleEllis titleDale EllisDale Ellisa returned to Seattle. Denver flirted with history in the a hrefwiki1997E2809398NBAseason title199798 NBA season199798a by nearly setting the mark for fewest wins in an 82game season 11. They tied the thenNBAs alltime worst isingleseasoni losing streak at a hrefwikiListofNationalBasketballAssociationlongestlosingstreaks titleList of National Basketball Association longest losing streaks23aonly one game shy of the overall worst mark of 24 by the a hrefwikiClevelandCavaliers titleCleveland CavaliersCleveland Cavaliersa of the early 1980s. The losing streak was later broken by the Cavaliers in 2011 and the a hrefwikiPhiladelphia76ers titlePhiladelphia 76ersPhiladelphia 76ersa in 2014 with 26 consecutive losses. Several years later the Nuggets tied for the worst record in the NBA in a hrefwiki2002E2809303NBAseason title200203 NBA season200203a also with the Cavaliers.
p
h4span classmwheadline idNewownershipsNew ownershipsspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection11 titleEdit section New ownershipseditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh4
pThe teams struggles in the late 1990s were due in part to ownership instability. COMSAT bought the a hrefwikiNationalHockeyLeague titleNational Hockey LeagueNHLas a hrefwikiQuebecNordiques titleQuebec NordiquesQuebec Nordiquesa in 1995 and moved them to Denver as the a hrefwikiColoradoAvalanche titleColorado AvalancheColorado Avalanchea. However its diversification into sports ownership was proving a drain on the company. In particular cost overruns associated with the construction of Pepsi Center had shareholders up in arms. Finally in 1997 COMSAT agreed in principle to sell Ascent Entertainment Group the umbrella corporation for its sporting assets to a hrefwikiLibertyMedia titleLiberty MediaLiberty Mediaa.sup idciterefnuggetscompanyhistory122 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggetscompanyhistory12911293asup However Liberty was not interested in sports ownership at the time though it has since bought the a hrefwikiAtlantaBraves titleAtlanta BravesAtlanta Bravesa and made the deal contingent upon Ascent selling the Avalanche and Nuggets.sup idciteref18 classreferencea hrefcitenote18911893asup
ppAfter almost two years Ascent sold the Avalanche and Nuggets to a hrefwikiWalmart titleWalmartWalmarta heirs a hrefwikiNancyWaltonLaurie titleNancy Walton LaurieBill and Nancy Lauriea for 400 million. However a group of Ascent shareholders sued claiming that the sale price was several million dollars too low. Ascent then agreed to sell the Avalanche and Nuggets to Denver banking tycoon Donald Sturm for 461 million.sup idciterefPress190 classreferencea hrefcitenotePress19911993asup
ppHowever a new wrinkle appeared when the city of Denver refused to transfer the parcel of land on which Pepsi Center stood unless Sturm promised to keep the Avalanche and Nuggets in Denver for at least 25 years. Sturm had bought the teams in his own name and the city wanted to protect itself in case Sturm either died or sold the teams before the 25 years ran out. While Sturm was willing to make a longterm commitment to the city he was not willing to be held responsible if he died or sold the teams. After negotiations fell apart Liberty bought all of Ascent but kept the Nuggets and Avalanche on the market.sup idciterefbizjournal200 classreferencea hrefcitenotebizjournal20912093asup In the meantime Issel had returned as head coach in 1999 but the protracted ownership negotiations made it difficult for him to rebuild the team. Just before the start of the 19992000 season he told reporters there were several personnel moves he simply could not make due to the unstable ownership situation since all basketball decisions required the approval of both AscentLiberty iandi Sturm.sup idciteref21 classreferencea hrefcitenote21912193asup
ppFinally in July 2000 the Avalanche Nuggets and Pepsi Center were bought by real estate entrepreneur a hrefwikiStanKroenke titleStan KroenkeStan Kroenkea in a 450 million deal.sup idciterefnuggetscompanyhistory123 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggetscompanyhistory12911293asup Kroenke is the brotherinlaw of the Lauries his wife a hrefwikiAnnWaltonKroenke titleAnn Walton KroenkeAnna is Nancy Lauries sister. Liberty retained only a 6.5 stake of the sports franchises. As part of the deal Kroenke placed the teams into a trust that would ensure the teams will stay in Denver until at least 2025.sup idciterefbizjournal201 classreferencea hrefcitenotebizjournal20912093asup After the deal Kroenke organized his sports assets under a hrefwikiKroenkeSportsEnterprises classmwredirect titleKroenke Sports EnterprisesKroenke Sports Enterprisesa.
p
h3span id2003.E2.80.932013GeorgeKarlinchargespanspan classmwheadline id20032013GeorgeKarlincharge20032013 George Karl in chargespanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection12 titleEdit section 20032013 George Karl in chargeeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
h4span id2003.E2.80.932006CarmeloAnthonyeraspanspan classmwheadline id20032006CarmeloAnthonyera20032006 Carmelo Anthony eraspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection13 titleEdit section 20032006 Carmelo Anthony eraeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh4
div classthumb trightdiv classthumbinner stylewidth222pxa hrefwikiFileCarmeloAnthonyNuggets.jpg classimageimg alt srcupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb33fCarmeloAnthonyNuggets.jpg220pxCarmeloAnthonyNuggets.jpg decodingasync width220 height378 classthumbimage srcsetupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb33fCarmeloAnthonyNuggets.jpg330pxCarmeloAnthonyNuggets.jpg 1.5x upload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb33fCarmeloAnthonyNuggets.jpg440pxCarmeloAnthonyNuggets.jpg 2x datafilewidth1462 datafileheight2515 a  div classthumbcaptiondiv classmagnifya hrefwikiFileCarmeloAnthonyNuggets.jpg classinternal titleEnlargeadivDenver drafted Carmelo Anthony third overall in the 2003 draft.divdivdiv
pIn a hrefwiki2003E2809304NBAseason title200304 NBA season2003a the Nuggets drafted future a hrefwikiNBAAllStarGame titleNBA AllStar GameAllStara a hrefwikiCarmeloAnthony titleCarmelo AnthonyCarmelo Anthonya with the third overall pick in the a hrefwiki2003NBAdraft title2003 NBA draft2003 NBA drafta.sup idciteref22 classreferencea hrefcitenote22912293asup That same year the team also updated their logos and uniforms with a new color scheme of powder blue gold and royal blue the latter color was changed to navy blue in 2008.sup idciteref23 classreferencea hrefcitenote23912393asup In just two months of the season the Nuggets recorded more wins than they had in 5 months of play in 200203. Much of the reason for this incredible turnaround were the frontoffice moves of a hrefwikiGeneralManager classmwredirect titleGeneral ManagerGeneral Managera a hrefwikiKikiVandeweghe classmwredirect titleKiki VandewegheKiki Vandeweghea a former Nuggets player who assumed General Manager duties on August 9 2001.sup idciterefkikinuggetsgm240 classreferencea hrefcitenotekikinuggetsgm24912493asup In April the turnaround was complete as they became the first franchise in NBA history to qualify for the postseason following a sub20win campaign the previous year since the NBA went to an 82game schedule.sup idciterefkikinuggetsgm241 classreferencea hrefcitenotekikinuggetsgm24912493asup They were eliminated in the first round 4 games to 1 by the a hrefwikiMinnesotaTimberwolves titleMinnesota TimberwolvesMinnesota Timberwolvesa.sup idciteref25 classreferencea hrefcitenote25912593asup
ppOn December 28 2004 head coach a hrefwikiJeffBzdelik titleJeff BzdelikJeff Bzdelika was fired from the organization and replaced by interim coach former a hrefwikiLosAngelesLakers titleLos Angeles LakersLos Angeles Lakersa player and a hrefwikiLosAngelesSparks titleLos Angeles SparksLos Angeles Sparksa head coach a hrefwikiMichaelCooper titleMichael CooperMichael Coopera.sup idciteref26 classreferencea hrefcitenote26912693asup The Nuggets later hired a hrefwikiGeorgeKarl titleGeorge KarlGeorge Karla as a permanent replacement.sup idciteref27 classreferencea hrefcitenote27912793asup Karl led the team to a record of 328 in the second half of the regular season which vaulted the team into the playoffs for the second consecutive year.sup idciteref28 classreferencea hrefcitenote28912893asup
ppIn the a hrefwiki2005NBAPlayoffs classmwredirect title2005 NBA Playoffsplayoffsa however the Nuggets could not survive the a hrefwikiSanAntonioSpurs titleSan Antonio SpursSan Antonio Spursa. After winning game one in a hrefwikiSanAntonioTexas classmwredirect titleSan Antonio TexasSan Antonioa the Nuggets proceeded to lose the next four games and lost the series 41.sup idciteref29 classreferencea hrefcitenote29912993asup The Nuggets picked 20th in the a hrefwiki2005NBAdraft title2005 NBA draft2005 NBA drafta it was acquired from the a hrefwikiWashingtonWizards titleWashington WizardsWashington Wizardsa via the a hrefwikiOrlandoMagic titleOrlando MagicOrlando Magica.sup idciteref2005NBADraft300 classreferencea hrefcitenote2005NBADraft30913093asup Denver selected a hrefwikiJuliusHodge titleJulius HodgeJulius Hodgea with the pick. The Nuggets also had the 22nd overall selection in the draft in which they selected a hrefwikiJarrettJack titleJarrett JackJarrett Jacka but sent him to the a hrefwikiPortlandTrailBlazers titlePortland Trail BlazersPortland Trail Blazersa for rights to Portlands 27th overall pick a hrefwikiLinasKleiza titleLinas KleizaLinas Kleizaa.sup idciteref2005NBADraft301 classreferencea hrefcitenote2005NBADraft30913093asup
ppIn a hrefwiki2005E2809306NBAseason title200506 NBA season200506a for the first time in 18 years the club won the Northwest division title.sup idciteref31 classreferencea hrefcitenote31913193asup This placed the team in the third seed of the Western Conference a hrefwiki2006NBAPlayoffs classmwredirect title2006 NBA Playoffsplayoffsa. Denver played the a hrefwikiLosAngelesClippers titleLos Angeles ClippersLos Angeles Clippersa who despite their 6th seeding had a better regularseason record. As a result the Clippers received home court advantage. They defeated the Nuggets in 5 games. Shortly after the Nuggets announced that General Manager Kiki Vandeweghes contract would not be renewed. He was replaced by a hrefwikiMarkWarkentien titleMark WarkentienMark Warkentiena.sup idciteref32 classreferencea hrefcitenote32913293asup
ppOn December 18 2006 team cocaptain a hrefwikiCarmeloAnthony titleCarmelo AnthonyCarmelo Anthonya shooting guard a hrefwikiJ.R.Smith titleJ. R. SmithJ. R. Smitha and power forward a hrefwikiNenC3AA titleNenNena were suspended by the NBA 15 10 and one games respectively for a a hrefwikiKnicksE28093Nuggetsbrawl titleKnicksNuggets brawlfighta that occurred in the last two minutes of a game against the a hrefwikiNewYorkKnicks titleNew York KnicksNew York Knicksa two days earlier.sup idciteref33 classreferencea hrefcitenote33913393asupsup idciteref34 classreferencea hrefcitenote34913493asup The fight was sparked by Knicks rookie a hrefwikiMardyCollins titleMardy CollinsMardy Collinsa when he tackled J. R. Smith on a breakaway layup. According to Anthony Knicks coach a hrefwikiIsiahThomas titleIsiah ThomasIsiah Thomasa warned him to not go in the paint shortly before the hard foul.sup idciteref35 classreferencea hrefcitenote35913593asup

h4span id2006.E2.80.932008AnthonyandIversonspanspan classmwheadline id20062008AnthonyandIverson20062008 Anthony and Iversonspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection14 titleEdit section 20062008 Anthony and Iversoneditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh4
div classthumb tleftdiv classthumbinner stylewidth222pxa hrefwikiFileIversonfrombehind.jpg classimageimg alt srcupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb889Iversonfrombehind.jpg220pxIversonfrombehind.jpg decodingasync width220 height300 classthumbimage srcsetupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb889Iversonfrombehind.jpg330pxIversonfrombehind.jpg 1.5x upload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb889Iversonfrombehind.jpg440pxIversonfrombehind.jpg 2x datafilewidth752 datafileheight1024 a  div classthumbcaptiondiv classmagnifya hrefwikiFileIversonfrombehind.jpg classinternal titleEnlargeadivAllen Iverson helped Denver to their first 50win season since 1988.divdivdiv
pOn December 19 2006 the Nuggets traded a hrefwikiJoeSmithbasketball titleJoe Smith basketballJoe Smitha a hrefwikiAndreMiller titleAndre MillerAndre Millera and two firstround draft picks of the a hrefwiki2007NBAdraft title2007 NBA draft2007 NBA drafta to the a hrefwikiPhiladelphia76ers titlePhiladelphia 76ersPhiladelphia 76ersa for a hrefwikiIvanMcFarlin titleIvan McFarlinIvan McFarlina and superstar a hrefwikiAllenIverson titleAllen IversonAllen Iversona McFarlin was waived immediately following the trades approval. The moves gave the Nuggets the top two scorers in the league at the time in Anthony and Iverson who were both scoring over 30 points per game at the time of the trade. On January 11 2007 a hrefwikiEarlBoykins titleEarl BoykinsEarl Boykinsa a hrefwikiJuliusHodge titleJulius HodgeJulius Hodgea and cash considerations were traded to the a hrefwikiMilwaukeeBucks titleMilwaukee BucksMilwaukee Bucksa in exchange for point guard a hrefwikiSteveBlake titleSteve BlakeSteve Blakea. With Iverson many considered the Nuggets as one of the elite in the West. However chemistry was an issue as the Nuggets finished the season with the 6 seed giving them a first round matchup against the a hrefwikiSanAntonioSpurs titleSan Antonio SpursSan Antonio Spursa. In the a hrefwiki2007NBAPlayoffs classmwredirect title2007 NBA Playoffsplayoffsa the Nuggets took Game 1 and home court advantage away from the Spurs. However as had occurred in the 2005 playoffs the Spurs bounced back to sweep the next four as the Nuggets were eliminated in the first round in five games for the fourth straight year.
ppOn March 16 a hrefwiki2007E2809308NBAseason title200708 NBA season2008a the Nuggets scored 168 points in a 168116 home win over a hrefwikiSeattleSuperSonics titleSeattle SuperSonicsSeattle SuperSonicsa.sup idciterefnuggets168points360 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggets168points36913693asup It was the thirdmost points scored for a regulation game in NBA history The Nuggets and the Pistons hold the spot for most combined points scored in a game which was over 360 points total.sup idciterefnuggets168points361 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggets168points36913693asup
ppThey finished the a hrefwiki2007E2809308NBAseason title200708 NBA season200708 NBA seasona with exactly 50 wins as well as finishing the first half of that season 2516 5032 overall record tied for the thirdbest alltime Nuggets record since the team officially joined the NBA in 1976 following a 120111 home victory over the a hrefwikiMemphisGrizzlies titleMemphis GrizzliesMemphis Grizzliesa in the last game of the season.sup idciterefnuggets50wins0708370 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggets50wins070837913793asup It was the first time since the a hrefwiki1987E2809388NBAseason title198788 NBA season198788 NBA seasona that the Nuggets finished with at least 50 wins in a season.sup idciterefnuggets50wins0708371 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggets50wins070837913793asup Denver ended up as the 8th seed in the Western Conference of the a hrefwiki2008NBAPlayoffs classmwredirect title2008 NBA Playoffs2008 NBA Playoffsa and their 50 wins marked the highest win total for an 8th seed in NBA history.sup idciterefnuggets50wins0708372 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggets50wins070837913793asup It also meant that for the first time in NBA history all eight playoff seeds in a Conference had at least 50 wins. The Nuggets faced the topseeded a hrefwikiLosAngelesLakers titleLos Angeles LakersLos Angeles Lakersa 5725 in the first round. The seven games separating the Nuggets and the Lakers overall records is the closest margin between an eighth seed and a top seed since the NBA went to a 16team playoff format in a hrefwiki1983E2809384NBAseason title198384 NBA season198384a.sup idciterefnuggets50wins0708373 classreferencea hrefcitenotenuggets50wins070837913793asup However the Lakers swept them in four games marking the second time in NBA history that a 50win team was swept in a a hrefwikiBestofsevenplayoff classmwredirect titleBestofseven playoffbestofseven playoff seriesa in the first round. It was Denvers fifth straight firstround loss.sup idciteref38 classreferencea hrefcitenote38913893asupsup idciteref39 classreferencea hrefcitenote39913993asup

h4span id2008.E2.80.932011AnthonyandBillupsspanspan classmwheadline id20082011AnthonyandBillups20082011 Anthony and Billupsspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection15 titleEdit section 20082011 Anthony and Billupseditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh4

ppOn November 3 2008 guard a hrefwikiAllenIverson titleAllen IversonAllen Iversona was traded to the a hrefwikiDetroitPistons titleDetroit PistonsDetroit Pistonsa for a hrefwikiChaunceyBillups titleChauncey BillupsChauncey Billupsa a hrefwikiAntonioMcDyess titleAntonio McDyessAntonio McDyessa and a hrefwikiCheikhSamb titleCheikh SambCheikh Samba part of the trade exception from the Marcus Camby trade was used to allow the deal to go through. div classthumb trightdiv classthumbinner stylewidth222pxa hrefwikiFileChaunceyBillupswiththeball.jpg classimageimg alt srcupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb00fChaunceyBillupswiththeball.jpg220pxChaunceyBillupswiththeball.jpg decodingasync width220 height293 classthumbimage srcsetupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb00fChaunceyBillupswiththeball.jpg330pxChaunceyBillupswiththeball.jpg 1.5x upload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb00fChaunceyBillupswiththeball.jpg440pxChaunceyBillupswiththeball.jpg 2x datafilewidth1758 datafileheight2345 a  div classthumbcaptiondiv classmagnifya hrefwikiFileChaunceyBillupswiththeball.jpg classinternal titleEnlargeadivChauncey Billups acquired in 2008 helped the George Karl Carmelo Anthony duo to their first playoff series win.divdivdiv
pWith a hrefwikiCarmeloAnthony titleCarmelo AnthonyCarmelo Anthonya averaging 22.8 points per game and Billups averaging 6.4 assists in the a hrefwiki2008E2809309NBAseason title200809 NBA season200809 NBA seasona the a hrefwiki2008E2809309DenverNuggetsseason title200809 Denver Nuggets seasonNuggetsa accomplished a great number of franchise milestones. Their 5428 record matched the most wins the franchise had gotten since their induction in the NBA their 2714 start was also a record for wins in the first half of a season. This also marked the first time in the franchises history the team had backtoback 50win seasons. They led the Northwest division for much of the season eventually winning the division and placing 2 in the Western Conference matching the highest the team has ever been seeded for the playoffs. a hrefwikiGeneralManager classmwredirect titleGeneral ManagerGeneral Managera a hrefwikiMarkWarkentien titleMark WarkentienMark Warkentiena won the a hrefwikiNBAExecutiveoftheYearAward titleNBA Executive of the Year AwardNBA Executive of the Year Awarda for the Nuggets improvement. They won Game 1 of the playoffs in a blowout victory against the a hrefwiki2008E2809309NewOrleansHornetsseason title200809 New Orleans Hornets seasonNew Orleans Hornetsa the first time they had homecourt advantage since a hrefwiki1987E2809388NBAseason title198788 NBA season1988a and also the 29point victory was the largest victory for any team for Game 1 of the first round of the a hrefwiki2009NBAPlayoffs classmwredirect title2009 NBA Playoffs2009 NBA Playoffsa. Chauncey Billups set a Nuggets franchise record with the most threepointers in a playoff game with 8 and his 19 threepointers in total is also a Nuggets record for threes made in a playoff series.sup idciteref40 classreferencea hrefcitenote40914093asup They went on to beat the Hornets in 5 including a 58point victory in Game 4 which matched the most lopsided win in a hrefwikiNBApostseasonrecords titleNBA postseason recordsNBA playoff historya. They then went on to beat the 6th seed a hrefwikiDallasMavericks titleDallas MavericksDallas Mavericksa 4 games to 1 in the Conference Semifinals to make their first trip to the a hrefwiki1985NBAPlayoffs classmwredirect title1985 NBA PlayoffsWestern Conference Finals since 1985a. That was also the first time the Nuggets had ever led 30 in a bestofseven series. Up to that point they held an NBA Playoffshigh in threepointers made and a 16point average margin of victory the largest average margin of victory in the first 10 playoff games in NBA Playoff history. They lost the first game of the Western Conference Finals against the a hrefwikiLosAngelesLakers titleLos Angeles LakersLos Angeles Lakersa but won the second game to tie the series. Anthony became the first Denver player to score at least 30 points in five consecutive playoff games since the Nuggets joined the NBA in 1976. They lost the series 42 ending Denvers longest playoff run in team history.sup idciteref41 classreferencea hrefcitenote41914193asup
ppIn the a hrefwiki2009NBAdraft title2009 NBA draft2009 NBA drafta the Nuggets traded a firstround draft pick acquired from the a hrefwikiCharlotteBobcats classmwredirect titleCharlotte BobcatsCharlotte Bobcatsa to the a hrefwikiMinnesotaTimberwolves titleMinnesota TimberwolvesMinnesota Timberwolvesa for the rights to rookie a hrefwikiTyLawson titleTy LawsonTy Lawsona who was drafted 18th overall. On July 13 2009 the Nuggets traded a secondround draft pick to the Detroit Pistons for a hrefwikiArronAfflalo titleArron AfflaloArron Afflaloa part of the trade exception from the Iverson trade was used to allow the deal to go through and a hrefwikiWalterSharpe titleWalter SharpeWalter Sharpea. Afflalo replaced starting guard a hrefwikiDahntayJones titleDahntay JonesDahntay Jonesa who signed with the a hrefwikiIndianaPacers titleIndiana PacersIndiana Pacersa.sup idciteref42 classreferencea hrefcitenote42914293asup However on August 10 the Nuggets lost forward a hrefwikiLinasKleiza titleLinas KleizaLinas Kleizaa who signed with a hrefwikiOlympiacosB.C. titleOlympiacos B.C.Olympiacos Piraeusa of the a hrefwikiA1Ethniki classmwredirect titleA1 EthnikiGreek Leaguea.sup idciteref43 classreferencea hrefcitenote43914393asup
ppThe a hrefwiki2009E2809310NBAseason title200910 NBA season200910 seasona saw Anthony average 28.2 points per game and Billups average a careerhigh 19.6 points per game. In the opening two games of the season Anthony totaled 71 points scoring 30 points in the home opener and 41 the next night in wins against division rivals a hrefwikiUtahJazz titleUtah JazzUtah Jazza and a hrefwikiPortlandTrailBlazers titlePortland Trail BlazersPortland Trail Blazersa respectively. Anthony became one of two players in the Nuggets history to open with more than 70 points through two games Alex English also accomplished the feat. It was also only the second time since 1987 that the Nuggets started the season 20.sup idciteref44 classreferencea hrefcitenote44914493asup They later went 30 40 and 50 for the first time since 1985 after defeating the a hrefwikiMemphisGrizzlies titleMemphis GrizzliesMemphis Grizzliesa a hrefwikiIndianaPacers titleIndiana PacersIndiana Pacersa and a hrefwikiNewJerseyNets classmwredirect titleNew Jersey NetsNew Jersey Netsa respectively. Despite injuries which caused all three captains  Carmelo Anthony Chauncey Billups and a hrefwikiKenyonMartin titleKenyon MartinKenyon Martina  to miss a total of 46 games and then later on in the second half of the season the absence of head coach a hrefwikiGeorgeKarl titleGeorge KarlGeorge Karla who underwent treatment for neck and a hrefwikiThroatcancer classmwredirect titleThroat cancerthroat cancera the Nuggets were still able to win 53 games third consecutive 50win season a Nuggets first for the season which gave them a second consecutive Northwest division title and finished as the fourth seed in the West Conference. However they were eliminated by the a hrefwikiUtahJazz titleUtah JazzUtah Jazza 42 their sixth firstround elimination in 7 seasons. Anthony averaged a careerhigh 30.7 points per game in the playoffs.
ppOn July 14 2010 the Nuggets bolstered their frontcourt depth by signing a hrefwikiAlHarrington titleAl HarringtonAl Harringtona.sup idciteref45 classreferencea hrefcitenote45914593asup During the 2010 offseason a hrefwikiMasaiUjiri titleMasai UjiriMasai Ujiria replaced a hrefwikiMarkWarkentien titleMark WarkentienMark Warkentiena as the General Manager while Josh Kroenke was named team president.
ppStan Kroenke bought full ownership in the thena hrefwikiHistoryoftheSt.LouisRams titleHistory of the St. Louis RamsSt. Louis Ramsa of the NFL in 2010. Since the NFL does not allow its owners to hold majority control of majorleague teams in other NFL cities Kroenke turned over daytoday control of the Nuggets and Avalanche to Josh Kroenke toward the end of 2010 and transferred his controlling interest in both teams to his wife in 2015.sup idciteref46 classreferencea hrefcitenote46914693asupsup idciteref47 classreferencea hrefcitenote47914793asup

h4span id2011.E2.80.932012Anthony.27sdeparturespanspan classmwheadline id20112012Anthonysdeparture20112012 Anthonys departurespanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection16 titleEdit section 20112012 Anthony039s departureeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh4
pOn February 22 2011 after months of speculation that he wanted to leave the Nuggets a hrefwikiCarmeloAnthony titleCarmelo AnthonyCarmelo Anthonya was traded along with a hrefwikiChaunceyBillups titleChauncey BillupsChauncey Billupsa a hrefwikiAnthonyCarter titleAnthony CarterAnthony Cartera a hrefwikiSheldenWilliams titleShelden WilliamsShelden Williamsa and a hrefwikiRenaldoBalkman titleRenaldo BalkmanRenaldo Balkmana to the a hrefwikiNewYorkKnicks titleNew York KnicksNew York Knicksa in a multiplayer deal also involving the a hrefwikiMinnesotaTimberwolves titleMinnesota TimberwolvesMinnesota Timberwolvesa in which the Nuggets received a hrefwikiWilsonChandler titleWilson ChandlerWilson Chandlera a hrefwikiRaymondFelton titleRaymond FeltonRaymond Feltona a hrefwikiDaniloGallinari titleDanilo GallinariDanilo Gallinaria a hrefwikiTimofeyMozgov titleTimofey MozgovTimofey Mozgova and a hrefwikiKostaKoufos titleKosta KoufosKosta Koufosa. On the day when the trade was done the Nuggets were left with 9 players to play against the a hrefwikiMemphisGrizzlies titleMemphis GrizzliesMemphis Grizzliesa. The Nuggets won 120107 where they led by as many as 27 points. In the closing minutes of the game the arena resounded with chants of Who needs Melo? George Karl said after the game Our guys when their backs are confronted with a difficult situation they usually play at a high level. We always react to tough situations in a very positive way. Some peoplesup classnoprint InlineTemplate stylewhitespacenowrap91ia hrefwikiWikipediaManualofStyleWordstowatchUnsupportedattributions titleWikipediaManual of StyleWords to watchspan titleThe material near this tag possibly uses toovague attribution or weasel words. June 2015who?spanai93sup said after the trade the Nuggets would become the a hrefwikiClevelandCavaliers titleCleveland CavaliersCleveland Cavaliersa of the West that is falter in the standings and lose their playoff hopes due to the loss of their franchise player Carmelo. However the trade only seemed to make them better. Posttrade the Nuggets averaged 24.1 assists showing their newfound teamwork. The defense of the Nuggets also improved from allowing 105.2 points per game before the trade to 97.1 points per game for the remainder of the season. sup idciteref48 classreferencea hrefcitenote48914893asup Despite the franchise changing trade which saw eighteen different starting lineups through the whole season Denver finished with 50 wins fourth consecutive 50 win seasons for the first time in Nuggets history clinching the 5th seed of the Western Conference. They met the a hrefwikiOklahomaCityThunder titleOklahoma City ThunderOklahoma City Thundera in the first round of the playoffs and lost four games to one.

div classthumb trightdiv classthumbinner stylewidth222pxa hrefwikiFileGeorgeKarl.jpg classimageimg alt srcupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb33dGeorgeKarl.jpg220pxGeorgeKarl.jpg decodingasync width220 height360 classthumbimage srcsetupload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb33dGeorgeKarl.jpg330pxGeorgeKarl.jpg 1.5x upload.wikimedia.orgwikipediacommonsthumb33dGeorgeKarl.jpg440pxGeorgeKarl.jpg 2x datafilewidth974 datafileheight1594 a  div classthumbcaptiondiv classmagnifya hrefwikiFileGeorgeKarl.jpg classinternal titleEnlargeadivGeorge Karl was named NBA Coach of the Year in 2013 his final season in Denverdivdivdiv
pThe first full season of the postMelo Nuggets saw the steady rise of Danilo Gallinari who averaged 17 points 5.2 rebounds and 2.6 assists through the first 25 games of the season which resulted to the Nuggets best start through the first 20 games. But Gallinari was robbed off his best season by injuries to his ankle thumb and wrist. On March 15 2012 the Nuggets decided to make their team younger by trading a hrefwikiNenC3AA titleNenNena who had played the previous 9 seasons for Denver to the a hrefwikiWashingtonWizards titleWashington WizardsWashington Wizardsa for a hrefwikiJaValeMcGee titleJaVale McGeeJaVale McGeea.sup idciteref49 classreferencea hrefcitenote49914993asup In his first game as a Nugget McGee made a putback dunk off an a hrefwikiArronAfflalo titleArron AfflaloArron Afflaloa miss which proved to be the gamewinning basket in Denvers 116115 victory over the Detroit Pistons. In two of the Nuggets final games of their season McGee finally earned national attention when he had a 16point15rebound effort and a 21point 14rebound effort in Denvers playoff series against the a hrefwikiLosAngelesLakers titleLos Angeles LakersLos Angeles Lakersa. These performances helped the Nuggets come back from a 20 and a 31 series deficit but the Nuggets eventually lost in Game 7 8796.

h4span id2012.E2.80.932013Teamconceptspanspan classmwheadline id20122013Teamconcept20122013 Team conceptspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection17 titleEdit section 20122013 Team concepteditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh4
pOn August 10 2012 Denver was involved in a fourteam trade where they received AllStar a hrefwikiAndreIguodala titleAndre IguodalaAndre Iguodalaa and sent Arron Afflalo and a hrefwikiAlHarrington titleAl HarringtonAl Harringtona to the a hrefwikiOrlandoMagic titleOrlando MagicOrlando Magica. This same trade also sent a hrefwikiDwightHoward titleDwight HowardDwight Howarda to the a hrefwikiLosAngelesLakers titleLos Angeles LakersLos Angeles Lakersa. After the trade Iguodala tweeted Im excited to be joining the Denver Nuggets and I know my best basketball is ahead of me!sup idciteref50 classreferencea hrefcitenote50915093asup Despite losing their first three games the 20122013 Nuggets finished with a franchise best 5725 record and a 383 record in Pepsi Center the Washington Wizards a hrefwikiMiamiHeat titleMiami HeatMiami Heata and Minnesota Timberwolves were the only 3 visitors to defeat Denver on their home during the regular season. Denver also clinched the 3rd seed in the Western Conference with a first round matchup with the a hrefwikiGoldenStateWarriors titleGolden State WarriorsGolden State Warriorsa. The Nuggets won Game 1 9795 on their home court on a last second Andre Miller game winner but the Warriors won the next three games putting the Nuggets on the brink of elimination. Denver won Game 5 at home to keep their season alive but the Warriors eliminated the Nuggets in Game 6 winning 8892 in Oakland. It was Denvers ninth first round loss in the previous 10 seasons and the eighth of Karls tenure. Although Karl won that years a hrefwikiNBACoachoftheYearAward titleNBA Coach of the Year AwardNBA Coach of the Year Awarda and had led Denver to the playoffs in every year of his nineyear tenure it was not enough to keep him from being fired after the season.

h3span id2013.E2.80.93presentspanspan classmwheadline id2013present2013presentspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection18 titleEdit section 2013presenteditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3

On June 21 2013 a hrefwikiTimConnelly titleTim ConnellyTim Connellya was announced as the new general manager.sup idciteref52 classreferencea hrefcitenote52915293asup and to replace Karl the Nuggets hired the Indiana Pacers associate head coach former NBA player a hrefwikiBrianShaw titleBrian ShawBrian Shawa. They also signed centerforward a hrefwikiJJHickson titleJJ HicksonJJ Hicksona who was previously with the Portland Trail Blazers and 5 9 guard a hrefwikiNateRobinson titleNate RobinsonNate Robinsona who played for the Bulls during the 20122013 season. ppUnder Michael Malones leadership the Denver Nuggets slightly started to improve while primarily relying on the youth movement consisting of Emmanuel Mudiay a hrefwikiNikolaJokiC487 titleNikola JokiNikola Jokia Gary Harris and later also on the recovered Jusuf Nurki. h2span idColors.2Clogosanduniformsspanspan classmwheadline idColorslogosanduniformsColors logos and uniformsspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection22 titleEdit section Colors logos and uniformseditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh2
pThe Nuggets have displayed numerous color schemes logos and uniforms throughout their franchise history including their days in the a hrefwikiAmericanBasketballAssociation titleAmerican Basketball AssociationAmerican Basketball Associationa ABA as the Denver Rockets.

h3span id1967.E2.80.931974DenverRockets.28ABA.29spanspan classmwheadline id19671974DenverRocketsABA19671974 Denver Rockets ABAspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection23 titleEdit section 19671974 Denver Rockets ABAeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pFrom 196768 through 197071 the Denver Rockets logos uniforms and colors were black orange and white. From 197172 through 197374 the Rockets wore gold and purple Columbine blue uniforms and their logo featured a cartoonish rocket bouncing a gold and purple basketball with a purple and white snowcapped mountain in the background.sup idciteref64 classreferencea hrefcitenote64916493asup
p
h3span id1974.E2.80.931981MaxieTheMinerspanspan classmwheadline id19741981MaxieTheMiner19741981 Maxie The Minerspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection24 titleEdit section 19741981 Maxie The Minereditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pDuring the Nuggets final two seasons in the a hrefwikiAmericanBasketballAssociation titleAmerican Basketball AssociationABAa the teams logo featured a cartoonish miner known as Maxie The Miner with a large red beard a pick axe in one hand and a red and blue basketball in the other hand. When the Nuggets joined the a hrefwikiNationalBasketballAssociation titleNational Basketball AssociationNBAa in the a hrefwiki1976E2809377NBAseason title197677 NBA season197677a season they retained the pickaxe logo on their jerseys from the ABA days. The home uniforms feature Nuggets in red with a red pickaxe inside a blue oval and gold numbers with blue trim in front blue numbers and letters at the back. The road uniforms were blue with Denver in blue with a blue pickaxe in a red oval and gold numbers in front white numbers and letters at the back. The Nuggets simplified their uniforms following their inaugural season in the NBA. From 197782 their home uniforms were white with a Nuggets script written across the chest in a darker royal blue with gold trim around the script and jersey numbers. The royal blue away jersey had Denver written across the chest in white with gold trim. 
p
h3span id1981.E2.80.931993RainbowCitySkylinespanspan classmwheadline id19811993RainbowCitySkyline19811993 Rainbow City Skylinespanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection25 titleEdit section 19811993 Rainbow City Skylineeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pFrom a hrefwiki1981E2809382NBAseason title198182 NBA season198182a through a hrefwiki1992E2809393NBAseason title199293 NBA season199293a the Nuggets wore the Denver rainbow city skyline across the chest and back on both the home and away uniforms. Some fans also call the iconic 1980s logo the a hrefwikiTetris titleTetrisTetrisa logo due to the buildings that shadow the mountains on the logo which are in the shape of squares. The initial home uniforms were white with navy and green trim with Nuggets and the uniform number in gold with blue trim. The player names were written in block lettering and in a straight position. In 1985 they changed the shade of blue to royal and eliminated green and in 1986 changed the back numbers to royal blue. In 1991 coinciding with the debut of a hrefwikiDikembeMutombo titleDikembe MutomboDikembe Mutomboa the word Nuggets became white with royal blue and gold trim. The road uniforms were initially navy blue with green trim with Denver and the uniform number in white with gold trim before likewise changing it to royal blue with gold serifed block letters for player names in an arch royal blue in home uniforms. The font and Skyline logo have been used on alternate jerseys to this day with it being on the Nuggets Statement uniforms.
p
h3span id1993.E2.80.932003Navyblue.2Cdarkredandmetallicgoldspanspan classmwheadline id19932003Navybluedarkredandmetallicgold19932003 Navy blue dark red and metallic goldspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection26 titleEdit section 19932003 Navy blue dark red and metallic goldeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pFor the a hrefwiki1993E2809394NBAseason title199394 NBA season199394a season the Nuggets drastically changed their look with a navy blue metallic gold and wine color scheme on their uniforms. The rainbow city skyline which had been synonymous with the team since 1981 was replaced with a logo that featured a navy blue snowcapped mountain above an enlarged westernstyle Nuggets wordmark in metallic gold and a curved dark red ribbon with a Denver wordmark positioned in between the mountain and the Nuggets wordmark. The home jerseys had a Nuggets script in a modified version of the typeface Aachen across the chest in navy blue with dark red and metallic gold trim around the script and numbers while the navy blue away jerseys had the same script in metallic gold with dark red and white trim. The Nuggets wore these uniforms for a decade until the end of the a hrefwiki2002E2809303NBAseason title200203 NBA season200203a season.
p
h3span id2003.E2.80.932018Powderblue.2Cnavyblueandgoldspanspan classmwheadline id20032018Powderbluenavyblueandgold20032018 Powder blue navy blue and goldspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection27 titleEdit section 20032018 Powder blue navy blue and goldeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pFor the a hrefwiki2003E2809304NBAseason title200304 NBA season200304a season the Nuggets made another uniform change coinciding with a hrefwikiCarmeloAnthony titleCarmelo AnthonyCarmelo Anthonyas debut with a color scheme of powder blue gold yellow and royal blue. The primary logo featuring a snowcapped mountain curved ribbon with a Denver wordmark and an enlarged westernstyle Nuggets workmark isee previous sectioni was modified with the snowcapped mountain royal blue the ribbon powder blue and the Nuggets wordmark a golden yellow. Like the 1990s uniforms the Nuggets revised jerseys also had the Aachen typeface across the chest  it was Nuggets in powder blue with royal blue and gold trim on the home white jersey while the powder blue road jerseys had Denver in white with gold and royal blue trim. These jerseys along with the team logo were tweaked prior to the a hrefwiki2008E2809309NBAseason title200809 NBA season200809a season with the royal blue replaced by the shade of navy blue that had been part of the teams color scheme from 19932003. These jerseys were used until the a hrefwiki2014E2809315NBAseason title201415 NBA season201415a season while the snowcapped mountain logo would serve as the teams primary logo until the a hrefwiki2017E2809318NBAseason title201718 NBA season201718a season.
ppIn the a hrefwiki2005E2809306NBAseason title200506 NBA season200506a season the Nuggets also introduced an alternate logo as well as an alternate navy blue uniform. The alternate logo featured twin intersecting gold pick axes in a powder blue circle with a gold nugget at the top of the circle and a basketball with gold outlining and navy blue accents. The navy blue jersey featured an alternate Nuggets script in gold with navy blue interior trim and powder blue outlining. This uniform was used until the end of the a hrefwiki2011E2809312NBAseason title201112 NBA season201112a season while the circular pick axe logo would become the teams new primary logo for the a hrefwiki2018E2809319NBAseason title201819 NBA season201819a season  isee next sectioni.
ppFor the a hrefwiki2012E2809313NBAseason title201213 NBA season201213a season the Nuggets unveiled a gold alternate jersey replacing the aforementioned navy blue jerseys that had been used during the previous seven seasons. This jersey featured a return to the Denver rainbow skyline logo but used the teams Aachen typeface and color scheme of powder blue navy and gold.sup idciteref65 classreferencea hrefcitenote65916593asup
ppFor the a hrefwiki2015E2809316NBAseason title201516 NBA season201516a season the Nuggets modified the script and numbering fonts on their home and away jerseys with a gold Nuggets script on the home white jersey and a gold Denver script on the powder blue away jersey  both with the Coliseum typeface. Navy blue numerals trimmed in gold as well as navy blue nameplates were featured on both the home and away jerseys. The alternate gold skyline jerseys were also tweaked with a retro Nuggets wordmark that was used on the 1980s rainbow skyline jerseys in navy blue trimmed in white. The numerals were also modified with the Coliseum typeface but remained white with powder blue interior trim and navy blue exterior outlining.sup idciteref66 classreferencea hrefcitenote66916693asup
ppThe Nuggets updated their uniforms for the 201718 season. The light uniform dubbed by a hrefwikiNikeInc. titleNike Inc.Nikea as the Association jersey the dark uniform dubbed by Nike as the Icon jersey and the alternate uniform dubbed by Nike as the Statement jersey saw the return of navy blue as a primary color for the first time since the 200203 season while powder blue was relegated to trim color status. Slight tweaks were made to the striping and lettering.sup idciteref67 classreferencea hrefcitenote67916793asupsup idciteref68 classreferencea hrefcitenote68916893asup The Nuggets gold Statement jersey made some noticeable alterations as well relegating the navy powder and white rainbow to the sides and relocating the number to the bottom. a hrefwikiWesternUnion titleWestern UnionWestern Uniona became the teams jersey sponsor.
p
h3span id2018.E2.80.93presentEvolvednewidentityspanspan classmwheadline id2018presentEvolvednewidentity2018present Evolved new identityspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection28 titleEdit section 2018present Evolved new identityeditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pFor the a hrefwiki2018E2809319NBAseason title201819 NBA season201819a season the Nuggets modified their logos and uniforms featuring various color schemes that the team has worn in their history. The new color scheme consists of midnight blue navy sunshine yellow flatirons red maroon and skyline blue royal  the latter color is only featured on the Statement jersey and two of the teams new alternate logos. Powder blue which had been part of the teams color scheme since 2003 was eliminated from all logos and uniforms. The white Association jersey features Nuggets in flatirons red with sunshine yellow trim and midnight blue numbers with sunshine yellow trim while the midnight blue Icon jersey features Denver in sunshine yellow with flatirons red trim and white numbers with flatirons red trim. Both sets will also include a mountain peak striping on the shorts and the pick axe logo on the waistline. The skyline blue Statement jersey features Mile High City in white surrounding sunshine yellow numbers plus a midnight blue mountain peak silhouette and a sunshine yellow pick axe logo on the sides of the shorts. A modernized version of the skyline logo adorns the waistline. The circular pick axe logo which had served as the Nuggets alternate logo since 2005 became the teams new primary logo replacing the snowcapped mountainenlarged westernstyle wordmark logo that had served as the teams primary logo in three different versions since 1993. The colors on the circular pick axe logo were also modified with the teams new color scheme.sup idciteref69 classreferencea hrefcitenote69916993asupsup idciteref70 classreferencea hrefcitenote70917093asup
p
h3span id.22City.22uniformsspanspan classmwheadline idquotCityquotuniformsCity uniformsspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection29 titleEdit section quotCityquot uniformseditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pIn the 201718 season a hrefwikiNikeInc. titleNike Inc.Nikea released a fourth uniform option known as the City series which is updated annually. The Nuggets first City uniform has a navy base highlighting the pickaxe and mountain logo in front and incorporating sublimated mountain peak patterns on the shorts.sup idciteref71 classreferencea hrefcitenote71917193asup
ppThe Nuggets 201819 City uniform was a callback to the teams 198293 rainbow uniforms featuring a sublimated pattern of the rainbow logo and navy lettering.sup idciteref72 classreferencea hrefcitenote72917293asup
p

h3span classmwheadline idRetaineddraftrightsRetained draft rightsspanspan classmweditsectionspan classmweditsectionbracketspana hrefwindex.php?titleDenverNuggetsampactioneditampsection32 titleEdit section Retained draft rightseditaspan classmweditsectionbracketspanspanh3
pThe Nuggets hold the draft rights to the following unsigned draft picks who have been playing outside the NBA. A drafted player either an international draftee or a college draftee who is not signed by the team that drafted him is allowed to sign with any nonNBA teams. In this case the team retains the players draft rights in the NBA until one year after the players contract with the nonNBA team ends.sup idciteref73 classreferencea hrefcitenote73917393asup This list includes draft rights that were acquired from trades with other teams.
p
